<user_id>111176201251067190462< /user_id><username>Ashley< /username>< date>
1512367206878</date>
<rating>2<//rating>< review>
I had been going here for about 4 years. If I had written this review 3 years into my regular visits, I would have given it 4 stars--tasty food but mediocre service.

So why the demotion to 2 stars?

This is my experience the last three times I've ordered takeout (I gave it the benefit of the doubt, but now I'm done):

1. Ordered a tofu curry. Got home and realized that they had given me the beef version of the curry. Had to drive back to get my proper order. Nothing comped for my troubles.

2. Ordered the same tofu curry. Checked that it was correct. Got home and on the last bite, bit into a chunk of...pork? chicken? Something definitely NOT tofu.

3. Ordered my usual tofu curry. Get home. Realize that there are small bits of shredded meat throughout my dish.

Sigh. Luckily, my tofu-love is not the result of a severe dietary restriction or rigid moral positions, but it was still incredibly distasteful to have meat in what was meant to be a meat-free dish.

I don't know what happened--a cook change? Lax quality control?--but after three times in a row, I just cannot justify going back, and this had been my favorite Thai place in town.

It has been a while since this experience, so hopefully they have fixed this issue, but I was severely disappointed with these problems and have not been back since.</review>

<gmap_id>0x808572d5961d0141:0x104fb9da48fc825e</gmap_id>< user_name>
E A< /user_name>
<rating>3< /rating>< review>
This spot is one of two Thai restaurants in Vallejo. It's good, to be sure, but when you've eaten at other Thai restaurants in the bay, it's not anything that's all that special in particular.

First and foremost, this place is probably one of the better spots in Vallejo if you're craving something that's in the realm of ethnic cuisine. The decor and overall environs of the restaurant are nice and clean. Almost a tropical feel to this place. Energy and vibe are great too. Some Friday nights, there's even local live music which is really nice. Staff here are consistently friend and helpful. Service is always fast, even when it's packed.

Now, the food itself. I've ordered the majority of the stuff on the menu within the 12 year span that I've been frequenting this place. Curries, pad thai, spicy dishes, grilled meats, and the seafoods. All of it? Good food and by no means bad at all. But having since also visited other Thai restaurants, I will say that the food here is not spectacular. But again, the food here is not bad at all. If you're local and not looking to set foot outside of the city, I would recommend this place (though Ano Thai Lao might be a better choice, depending on your location in the city.) This place is OK overall.</review>

<userid>116646067409953740906</userid>< review>
THE SHOP IS ON THE LEFT CORNER NEAR THE PARKING LOT! Very specialized shop for ukulele players.

Better than Guitar Center, in my opinion. Lots of high-end models/brands, accessories, and learning material.

Pretty much everything you need and a little more to get you started or to improve.

I walked in planning to purchase a 5 or 6 string tenor ukulele But walked out with a Kala Baritone. Amazing tone and projection. It was the sound I was looking for.

Before my purchase, I tried out a few 6 strings tenors and then a super tenor, and then a few  costing over $1,000. He helped me with my searching process and made excellent recommendations.

Highly recommended 5/5

Thank you Hale Ukulele!

Can't wait for COVID to be over so I can become more involved in the ukulele scene.< /review>

<Rate>2< /Rate>< Review>
I drove all the way from Las Vegas and purchased a 2016 Mercedes GLC300 from United Imports and my sales person's name is Lopez. He was pretty helpful and I had a overall great experience at the shop, despite having to wait here and there.

As I was driving home I noticed some weird noise coming from under the hood when I turn left or right. So I went to my local mercedes dealership and they found out the battery holder is completely MISSING! Also, the battery is not the correct size. I got a $750 quote from them to get it fixed. - new battery, battery holder and nuts. The mechanic also told me that he would not expect a reputed dealership to sell a car like this, since an undersized battery could cause potential electrical issues and alternator problems.

I understand the dealership had a sold as-is policy, but I was also handed a sheet that states the car has passed 21 inspections, which clearly include checking battery, cables, and terminals. This issue indicates the inspections was either not done at all, or not done properly.

The past few days I have been trying to call the shop but for the most time I couldn't get someone to answer. I texted the person who sold me the car but haven't got a response. Finally got my call answered and spoke to another sales person and he told me if I was in San Jose still he could swap out the battery for free. That was not a realistic option for me as I already drove back home. Then he told me to speak to manager Issac, I called his desk, left a voicemail but have not yet received a response.

I may update this review if someone follows up with me and come up with a solution. Otherwise I will leave it as a 2-star based on my poor post-sale experience.</Review>

Rolfe Horn< /Name>
< date>
1513286729121<//date>
< Rating>
5</Rating>
< review>
Great buying experience.

First off, I must say that I was skeptical because I tend to read the lowest reviews first.  Rolling back the odometer, misrepresenting Carfax reports and heavy-handed financing were my concern as I had looked over the BBB website complaints for United Imports of San Jose.

Samson Hague, the operations manager who handled my buying experience, was honest about the past issues after I had brought up my concerns.  I believe there were some misunderstandings from customers in the past.  Samson was very patient and polite, not at all aggressive or temperamental.  He is a delight to negotiate with.

I had brought with me a printed out copy of the free Carfax report of the car which I was interested in and he went to the Carfax website and immediately printed out the full report.  We both signed each page of the Carfax report saying that everything is accurate and true in the report (as reported by Carfax) has not been modified by any employee or staff of United Imports of San Jose.

After buying the car, I took it to my mechanic and everything checked out in the car and everything is as represented by Samson.

United Imports sold me my car for about $9000 less (30%+less) then a certified pre-owned vehicle of the same spec and mileage.  When I took the car home I did have to update the software in the car and will have to do some things that the dealer would normally do on a certified pre-owned vehicle.  The front tires will need replacing in about 7,000 miles, rear brakes in about 6,000 miles.  Somewhere in the neighborhood of $800 to fix/replace.  Not bad.

Basically, from my understanding, they buy most cars at auction as lease turn ins.  They detail the exterior, detail the interior, but leave the motor and undercarriage  original, which is good so you can see if fluids are leaking or not.  Certified and other  dealers clean everything so you don't know if the power steering pump dribbles
a bit or if the engine oil pan gasket seeps.  I liked the fact I could see the normal road dirt and not a single leak or speck of engine fluid.

This is as close as you can get to buying a car at auction yourself without having an auction license.  Wholesale plus a few hundred dollars.  Nice deal.

I did have to haggle on the interest to get it to where I felt it should be for my loan.  That is really the only place you can haggle, as the price for the car is fixed as the cars are much less expensive than certified pre-owned or other dealers.

All in all, I am totally satisfied with United Importers.  I went in with big time doubts, left happy but somewhat weary, (didn't get the car pre-checked) and after my independent service guy went over the car and told me it's all good, happy as a clam.

I'd recommend United Imports to anyone, whole heartedly.  Make sure you do your homework on the car first, as you should do with any used vehicle.  You will not be disappointed in the price you get from them, and you will wake up the next day thinking of how much money you saved by buying a car from them.< /review>

<UserId.>118134598177665827847<//UserId.><name>Kelsey Davis<//name>< date>
1600804742054< /date>
<rate>5< /rate>< Text>
I have so many good things to say about Seven Seas!

1. The coffee is great! My go-to is a dirty chai with oat milk. There's plenty of options when it comes to flavors, milk subs, etc.

2. The beans are roasted in-house; you can also buy bags there or order them online (the order online option really got us through a huge chunk of quarantine).

3. The baristas are awesome! Super welcoming, remember our names, remember our orders, and genuinely get to know the customers. They are also well-informed on coffee and offer suggestions if you aren't sure what to order.

4. Awesome atmosphere! South Park is great, and Seven Seas is right in the heart of it. The interior of the shop is cool too - check out the fish tank and custom art (when we can one day go inside again)! I love the garage-door style front.

5. This is one of my favorite things: they clearly have a great relationship and sense of community with the surrounding local businesses. They've gotten T-shirt designs done by the tattoo artists next door at Left Hand Black. They regularly set up at local farmers markets. There's often a local restaurant pop-up outside the shop on Sundays (sometimes other days too. They often have sweets from local bakeries like Matteo for sale. And during this weird time in 2020, they've offered the area in front of the shop to neighboring restaurant Piacere Mio for extra outdoor seating space during the evening.

Bonus: you can't come to Seven Seas without running into a cute dog, or several (and there's always a welcoming bowl of water out if you want to bring your pup too)!< /Text>
